data-track-component="pagecontent" data-type-tab="height" id="" class="marginBottom20 shadow24  carSummary readMoreLess " data-read-more="moveTop"><h2 class="">Grand Vitara Specs, Features and Price</h2><p id="model-highlight" class="gs_readmore marginBottom20 " style="height:48px">The <a href="/carmodels/Maruti/Maruti_Grand_Vitara" title="Grand Vitara">Maruti Grand Vitara</a> has 2 Petrol Engine and 1 CNG Engine on offer. The Petrol engine is 1462 cc and 1490 cc while the CNG engine is 1462 cc .  It is available with Manual  &  Automatic transmission.Depending upon the variant and fuel type the Grand Vitara has a mileage of 19.38 to 27.97 kmpl & Ground clearance of Grand Vitara is 210 mm. The Grand Vitara is a 5 seater <a href="/new-3-cylinder+cars" target="_blank">3 cylinder car</a>  and has length of 4345 mm, width of 1795 mm and a wheelbase of 2600 mm.</p><div class=" viewmore " Transmission</span></h3><table><tbody><tr><td class="">Engine Type<div class="tootTipCtr"><i class="icon-info tooltipIcon"></i><div class="tooltipDesc">Engine type in car refers to the type of engine that powers the vehicle. There are many different types of car engines, but the most common are petrol (gasoline) and diesel engines</div></div></td><td data-responsivecelltwo="true"><span>M15D With Strong Hybrid</span></td></tr><tr><td class="">Displacement<div class="tootTipCtr"><i class="icon-info tooltipIcon"></i><div class="tooltipDesc">The displacement of an engine is the total volume of all of the cylinders in the engine.
